I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Bug] False positive in pre-publish validator: function-call assignment to token variable is treated as leaked secret
### Summary

The pre-publish validator is producing a false positive for normal Python code that assigns a function return value to a variable named `token`. 

### Steps To Reproduce

  ### Current behavior

  Publishing fails with an error like:

  ```text
  Pre-publish validation failed:
  scripts/f2e_mock.py line 1842 contains a value that looks like a secret or token. Replace real credentials with placeholders before publishing.
```

  A representative line that triggers the error is:

  token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)

  This line does not contain a hardcoded credential. It only assigns the return value of a function call.

  ### Minimal example

  def maybe_generate_group_token(...):
      requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)
      ...
      token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)
      if token:
          return token
      ...

  ### Why this looks like a false positive

  The pre-publish validator currently uses a regex-based heuristic in:

  - server/skillhub-domain/src/main/java/com/iflytek/skillhub/domain/skill/validation/BasicPrePublishValidator.java

  Relevant rule:

  (?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})

  This regex scans text line-by-line and does not parse Python syntax. As a result:

  - the left-hand side matches token
  - the right-hand side matches the identifier prefix extract_group_token_value
  - the validator treats that identifier as a “secret-like value”

  So function calls / identifiers can be mistaken for leaked secrets.

  ### Related code path

  The validator is invoked during publish here:

  - server/skillhub-domain/src/main/java/com/iflytek/skillhub/domain/skill/service/SkillPublishService.java

  ### Expected behavior

  The validator should block obvious hardcoded credentials, but should not reject:

  - variable assignments
  - function-call return values
  - ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc.

  Example that should be allowed:

  token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)


### Expected Behavior

  ### Suggested regression test

  A test case similar to this should pass:

  token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)

  while real hardcoded secrets such as:

  token = "ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"
  api_key = "sk-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"

  should still fail.

### Environment

_No response_

### API Contract Impact

_No response_

### Logs Or Screenshots

_No response_

</pr_description>

     1	package com.iflytek.skillhub.domain.skill.validation;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     4	
     5	import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
     6	import java.util.ArrayList;
     7	import java.util.List;
     8	import java.util.Locale;
     9	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    10	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    11	
    12	/**
    13	 * Default pre-publish validator that scans text-like package files for likely secrets and
    14	 * accidental real credentials.
    15	 */
    16	@Component
    17	public class BasicPrePublishValidator implements PrePublishValidator {
    18	
    19	    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
    20	            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    21	    );
    22	    private static final List<SecretRule> SECRET_RULES = List.of(
    23	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16})"), 1, "cloud access key"),
    24	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(ghp_[A-Za-z0-9]{20,})"), 1, "GitHub token"),
    25	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(sk-[A-Za-z0-9]{20,})"), 1, "API key"),
    26	            new SecretRule(
    27	                    Pattern.compile("(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})"),
    28	                    2,
    29	                    "secret or token")
    30	    );
    31	
    32	    @Override
    33	    public ValidationResult validate(SkillPackageContext context) {
    34	        List<String> errors = new ArrayList<>();
    35	
    36	        for (PackageEntry entry : context.entries()) {
    37	            if (!isTextLike(entry.path())) {
    38	                continue;
    39	            }
    40	            String content = new String(entry.content(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    41	            String[] lines = content.split("\\R", -1);
    42	            for (int i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    43	                String line = lines[i];
    44	                for (SecretRule rule : SECRET_RULES) {
    45	                    Matcher matcher = rule.pattern().matcher(line);
    46	                    if (!matcher.find()) {
    47	                        continue;
    48	                    }
    49	                    String matchedValue = matcher.group(rule.valueGroup());
    50	                    if (isPlaceholderValue(matchedValue)) {
    51	                        continue;
    52	                    }
    53	                    errors.add(entry.path()
    54	                            + " line " + (i + 1)
    55	                            + " contains a value that looks like a "
    56	                            + rule.label()
    57	                            + ". Replace real credentials with placeholders before publishing.");
    58	                    break;
    59	                }
    60	            }
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        return errors.isEmpty() ? ValidationResult.pass() : ValidationResult.fail(errors);
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    private boolean isTextLike(String path) {
    67	        String lowerPath = path.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    68	        return lowerPath.endsWith(".md") || lowerPath.endsWith(".txt")
    69	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".json") || lowerPath.endsWith(".yaml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".yml")
    70	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".js") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ts")
    71	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".py") || lowerPath.endsWith(".sh") || lowerPath.endsWith(".svg")
    72	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".html") || lowerPath.endsWith(".css") || lowerPath.endsWith(".csv")
    73	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".toml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".xml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ini")
    74	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".cfg") || lowerPath.endsWith(".env")
    75	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".rb") || lowerPath.endsWith(".go") || lowerPath.endsWith(".rs")
    76	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".java") || lowerPath.endsWith(".kt") || lowerPath.endsWith(".lua")
    77	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".sql") || lowerPath.endsWith(".r")
    78	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".bat") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ps1")
    79	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".zsh") || lowerPath.endsWith(".bash");
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    private boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
    83	        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
    84	            return false;
    85	        }
    86	        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
    87	                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    private record SecretRule(Pattern pattern, int valueGroup, String label) {}
    91	}

Now I can see the issue clearly. The regex on line 27:

```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})
```

This regex matches things like:
- `token = extract_group_token_value(...)` where `token` is the left-hand assignment and `extract_group_token_value` (which has more than 12 characters) is treated as the value.

The problem is that the regex doesn't account for the fact that after the `=` sign, the value could be a function call (with parentheses), an identifier referring to another variable/function, etc.

2026-05-30 02:00:58,564 - INFO - swea-agent-iflytek__skillhub-253 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me understand the problem better. The regex on line 27:

```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})
```

For a line like:
```
token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)
```

The regex matches:
- `token` as the key
- `extract_group_token_value` as the value (since it's alphanumeric with underscores and has more than 12 chars)

The issue is that the regex doesn't consider that the value could be a function call (followed by `(`) or could be part of a larger expression.

Let me create a script to reproduce the issue

import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Reproduce {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Pattern pattern = Pattern.compile("(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})");
        
        String[] testLines = {
            "token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)",
            "token = \"ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx\"",
            "api_key = \"sk-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx\"",
            "token=YOUR_TOKEN_HERE",
            "password = some_function_call()",
            "secret = getSecretValue()",
            "token = some_var_name",
            "token = some_var_name_12345",
        };
        
        for (String line : testLines) {
            Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            System.out.println("Line: " + line);
            if (found) {
                System.out.println("  MATCHED! group1=" + matcher.group(1) + " group2=" + matcher.group(2));
            } else {
                System.out.println("  NOT matched");
            }
            System.out.println();
        }
    }
}
EOF

- `token = extract_group_token_value(...)` - should NOT be caught (it's a function call)

- `api_key = \"sk-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx\"` - should be caught

- `token = ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx` (without quotes in YAML, for example)

- Rules 1-3 (lines 23-25) already handle specific patterns like `AKIA...`, `ghp_...`, `sk-...`

Actually, let me re-read the PR. The minimal example shows:

```python
def maybe_generate_group_token(...):
    requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)
    ...
    token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)
    if token:
        return token
```

The line `token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)` is the one causing the false positive. The fix should ensure this doesn't match.

Let me look at the regex more carefully. The value `extract_group_token_value` matches `([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})`. The issue is that `extract_group_token_value` is followed by `(response, ...)` but the regex just grabs the identifier part.

So the simplest fix is to ensure that when the value is not quoted, it must not be immediately followed by `(` or `.` (for method calls) and should perhaps be at a word boundary.

Let me draft the fix:

Option 1: Add `(?!\s*\()` after the value group:
```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})(?!\s*\()
```

This prevents matching function calls. But `token = some_var` would still match.

Option 2: Make the regex require quotes for the value, OR require that the value ends at a word boundary and is not a function call. But that's complex.

Option 3: After the match, check if the matched value is followed by `(` in the line. This is what we could do in the Java code itself, not just the regex.

Let me go with the approach of modifying the regex to not match function calls (negative lookahead for `(`), and also add a check that if the value is unquoted and looks like just a plain identifier (which could be a variable reference), we should be more cautious.

But wait - the PR description says the expected behavior includes:

> Example that should be allowed:
> `token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)`

And:

> while real hardcoded secrets such as:
> `token = "ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"`
> `api_key = "sk-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"`
> should still fail.

So the key distinction is:
- Quoted strings → fail (catch)
- Function calls → allow
- Variable references → allow (based on "ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc.")

I think the best approach is to modify the regex so that:
1. If there's a quote before the value, we require the value to be followed by the closing quote
2. If there's no quote, the value must not be followed by `(` and should probably be at the end of the "token" (followed by space, comma, end of line, etc.)

But actually, looking at it more simply: the issue is just that `extract_group_token_value` matches because it's 12+ alphanumeric chars. If we add a negative lookahead for `(`, it won't match function calls anymore. Let me also consider that variable references like `some_variable` are also matched, but the PR says they should be allowed too.

Hmm, but if we allow all unquoted identifiers, then rule 4 becomes almost useless for unquoted values. Let me check what the other rules cover:
- Rule 1: `AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16}` - AWS access keys
- Rule 2: `ghp_[A-Za-z0-9]{20,}` - GitHub tokens
- Rule 3: `sk-[A-Za-z0-9]{20,}` - API keys

These specific patterns are already caught by rules 1-3. Rule 4 is a catch-all for other patterns like `password = something` or `secret = something`.

So maybe the fix should be more nuanced. Let me think about what legitimate secrets look like:
- `password = "mySecret123"`
- `secret: "abc123def456"`
- `token = "ya29.xxxxx"` (Google OAuth token)
- `api_key = "1234567890abcdef"`

And what false positives look like:
- `token = extract_group_token_value(...)` (function call)
- `token = some_variable`
- `password = get_password()`

I think the most robust fix is to modify the regex to only match when:
1. The value is properly quoted (both opening and closing quotes present)
2. OR the value is not followed by `(` (not a function call) AND not followed by a dot (not a method chain)

But there's another issue: `token = some_variable_name` where `some_variable_name` is a Python variable. How do we distinguish from a hardcoded secret?

One approach: if the value is unquoted, it should only be flagged if it looks "random enough" (has mixed case, numbers, etc.) which is more typical of secrets than variable names. But that's complex.

Let me look at what the actual fix should be by considering the PR description again:

> The validator should block obvious hardcoded credentials, but should not reject:
> - variable assignments
> - function-call return values
> - ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc.

So they want to allow all unquoted identifiers. This would mean rule 4 should ONLY match quoted values (or values that match specific patterns like rules 1-3).

So maybe the fix for rule 4 is simply to require quotes around the value? Let me check:

- `token = extract_group_token_value(...)` → NOT caught (no quotes)

But actually, I think the better approach is to add a negative lookahead for `(` to prevent function call matching, and also to check if the value looks like it could be a function/variable reference by checking if it's followed by `(` or if the line after the value contains more code-like syntax.

Let me take the simplest effective approach: modify the regex to not match when the captured value is followed by `(`. This directly addresses the reported bug.

Additionally, I should also consider the case where the value is followed by a dot (method calls like `obj.method`), but the character class `[A-Za-z0-9_\-]` already doesn't include dots, so the match would stop at the dot.

Wait, let me re-check. For `token = obj.method()`, the regex would match `obj` (if `obj` is 12+ chars, unlikely) or `method` (if 12+ chars). Actually it would match `obj` since `obj` is only 3 chars, the minimum is 12. So it wouldn't match. Good.

For `token = some_module.some_function()`, `some_module` has 11 chars (no match), `some_function` has 13 chars but it's after a dot. The regex would start matching from after `= `, so it would try `some_module` first (11 chars, too short), then... actually the regex engine would try to match starting at `some_module` but `some_module` is only 11 chars, which doesn't meet the 12-char minimum. So it would find `some_function`? No, because the dot is not in the character class, so the regex can't skip over it. It would fail to match.

Actually, let me re-check. The regex is:
```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})
```

For `token = some_module.some_function()`:
- `token` matches group 1
- `\s*=\s*` matches ` = `
- `['\"]?` optionally matches a quote (none here)
- `([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})` tries to match at position after `= `. The first characters are `some_module` (11 chars), but it needs 12+. The regex engine might find a match later... but the `\s*[:=]\s*` already consumed ` = `, so the match attempt is anchored right after `= `. It tries `some_module` which is 11 chars (too short). Since there's no 12+ char match starting at that position, the match fails. Good.

So the only problematic case is when the function name (or variable name) itself is 12+ characters, like `extract_group_token_value`.

So the fix of adding `(?!\s*\()` after the value group should handle this.

Let me also consider: what if the line is `token = get_token()` - `get_token` is only 9 chars, so it wouldn't match anyway.

And `token = some_func()` - `some_func` is 9 chars, no match.

But there's also the case of variable references: `token = some_long_variable_name` (16 chars). According to the PR, this should be allowed too. But with just the negative lookahead for `(`, it would still match.

- `token = some_long_variable_name` (variable reference, should be allowed)

1. Add negative lookahead for `(` to prevent function call false positives

   122	    /**
   123	     * Publishes an extracted package into the target namespace.
   124	     *
   125	     * <p>Super administrators may auto-publish, while regular publishers
   126	     * usually create a pending-review version.
   127	     */
   128	    @Transactional
   129	    public PublishResult publishFromEntries(
   130	            String namespaceSlug,
   131	            List<PackageEntry> entries,
   132	            String publisherId,
   133	            SkillVisibility visibility,
   134	            java.util.Set<String> platformRoles) {
   135	        return publishFromEntriesInternal(namespaceSlug, entries, publisherId, visibility, platformRoles, false, false);
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    /**
   139	     * Rebuilds a new version from an already published version by copying its
   140	     * stored files and rewriting the embedded metadata version field.
   141	     */
   142	    @Transactional
   143	    public PublishResult rereleasePublishedVersion(
   144	            Long skillId,
   145	            String sourceVersion,
   146	            String targetVersion,
   147	            String publisherId,
   148	            Map<Long, NamespaceRole> userNamespaceRoles) {

   150	                .orElseThrow(() -> new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.notFound", skillId));
   151	        assertCanManageLifecycle(skill, publisherId, userNamespaceRoles);
   152

   154	                .orElseThrow(() -> new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.version.notFound", sourceVersion));
   155	        if (publishedVersion.getStatus() != SkillVersionStatus.PUBLISHED) {
   156	            throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.version.notPublished", sourceVersion);
   157	        }
   158	        if (skillVersionRepository.findBySkillIdAndVersion(skillId, targetVersion).isPresent()) {
   159	            throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.version.exists", targetVersion);
   160	        }

   163

   169	                Set.of(),

   173	    }
   174	
   175	    private PublishResult publishFromEntriesInternal(
   176	            String namespaceSlug,
   177	            List<PackageEntry> entries,
   178	            String publisherId,
   179	            SkillVisibility visibility,
   180	            Set<String> platformRoles,
   181	            boolean forceAutoPublish,
   182	            boolean bypassMembershipCheck) {
   183	
   184	        // 1. Find namespace by slug
   185	        Namespace namespace = namespaceRepository.findBySlug(namespaceSlug)
   186	                .orElseThrow(() -> new DomainBadRequestException("error.namespace.slug.notFound", namespaceSlug));
   187	        assertNamespaceWritable(namespace);
   188	
   189	        boolean isSuperAdmin = platformRoles.contains("SUPER_ADMIN");
   190	
   191	        // 2. Check publisher is member unless SUPER_ADMIN short-circuits permission checks
   192	        if (!isSuperAdmin && !bypassMembershipCheck) {
   193	            namespaceMemberRepository.findByNamespaceIdAndUserId(namespace.getId(), publisherId)
   194	                    .orElseThrow(() -> new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.publish.publisher.notMember", namespaceSlug));
   195	        }
   196	
   197	        // 3. Validate package
   198	        ValidationResult packageValidation = skillPackageValidator.validate(entries);
   199	        if (!packageValidation.passed()) {
   200	            throw new DomainBadRequestException(
   201	                    "error.skill.publish.package.invalid",
   202	                    String.join(", ", packageValidation.errors()));
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        // 4. Parse SKILL.md
   206	        PackageEntry skillMd = entries.stream()
   207	                .filter(e -> e.path().equals("SKILL.md"))
   208	                .findFirst()
   209	                .orElseThrow(() -> new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.publish.skillMd.notFound"));
   210	
   211	        String skillMdContent = new String(skillMd.content());
   212	        SkillMetadata metadata = skillMetadataParser.parse(skillMdContent);
   213	        if (metadata.version() == null || metadata.version().isBlank()) {
   214	            String autoVersion = AUTO_VERSION_FORMATTER.format(currentTime());
   215	            metadata = new SkillMetadata(metadata.name(), metadata.description(), autoVersion, metadata.body(), metadata.frontmatter());
   216	        }
   217	        String skillSlug = SlugValidator.slugify(metadata.name());
   218	
   219	        // 5. Run PrePublishValidator
   220	        PrePublishValidator.SkillPackageContext context = new PrePublishValidator.SkillPackageContext(
   221	                entries, metadata, publisherId, namespace.getId());
   222	        ValidationResult prePublishValidation = prePublishValidator.validate(context);
   223	        if (!prePublishValidation.passed()) {
   224	            throw new DomainBadRequestException(
   225	                    "error.skill.publish.precheck.failed",
   226	                    String.join(", ", prePublishValidation.errors()));
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        // 6. Find or create Skill record (with owner isolation)
   230	        List<Skill> existingSkills = skillRepository.findByNamespaceIdAndSlug(namespace.getId(), skillSlug);
   231	
   232	        // Check if any other owner's skill has published versions
   233	        for (Skill existing : existingSkills) {
   234	            if (!existing.getOwnerId().equals(publisherId)) {
   235	                boolean hasPublished = !skillVersionRepository
   236	                        .findBySkillIdAndStatus(existing.getId(), SkillVersionStatus.PUBLISHED)
   237	                        .isEmpty();
   238	                if (hasPublished) {
   239	                    throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.publish.nameConflict", skillSlug);
   240	                }
   241	            }
   242	        }
   243	
   244	        // Find or create skill for current user
   245	        Skill skill = skillRepository.findByNamespaceIdAndSlugAndOwnerId(namespace.getId(), skillSlug, publisherId)
   246	                .orElseGet(() -> {
   247	                    Skill newSkill = new Skill(namespace.getId(), skillSlug, publisherId, visibility);
   248	                    newSkill.setCreatedBy(publisherId);
   249	                    return skillRepository.save(newSkill);
   250	                });
   251	
   252	        if (skill.getStatus() == SkillStatus.ARCHIVED) {
   253	            throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.publish.archived", skillSlug);
   254	        }
   255	
   256	        // 6c. Auto-withdraw pending review versions
   257	        List<SkillVersion> pendingVersions = skillVersionRepository
   258	                .findBySkillIdAndStatus(skill.getId(), SkillVersionStatus.PENDING_REVIEW);
   259	        for (SkillVersion pending : pendingVersions) {
   260	            reviewTaskRepository.findBySkillVersionIdAndStatus(pending.getId(), ReviewTaskStatus.PENDING)
   261	                    .ifPresent(reviewTaskRepository::delete);
   262	            pending.setStatus(SkillVersionStatus.DRAFT);
   263	            skillVersionRepository.save(pending);
   264	        }
   265	
   266	        // 7. Check version doesn't already exist
   267	        java.util.Optional<SkillVersion> existingVersion = skillVersionRepository.findBySkillIdAndVersion(skill.getId(), metadata.version());
   268	        if (existingVersion.isPresent()) {
   269	            SkillVersion matchedVersion = existingVersion.get();
   270	            if (matchedVersion.getStatus() == SkillVersionStatus.PUBLISHED) {
   271	                throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.version.exists", metadata.version());
   272	            }
   273	            deleteReplaceableVersionArtifacts(skill, matchedVersion, namespaceSlug);
   274	        }
   275	
   276	        // 8. Create SkillVersion
   277	        SkillVersion version = new SkillVersion(skill.getId(), metadata.version(), publisherId);
   278	        version.setRequestedVisibility(visibility);
   279	        boolean autoPublish = forceAutoPublish || isSuperAdmin;
   280	        if (autoPublish) {
   281	            version.setStatus(SkillVersionStatus.PUBLISHED);
   282	            version.setPublishedAt(currentTime());
   283	        } else {
   284	            version.setStatus(SkillVersionStatus.PENDING_REVIEW);
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        // Store metadata as JSON
   288	        try {
   289	            String metadataJson = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(metadata);
   290	            version.setParsedMetadataJson(metadataJson);
   291	            version.setManifestJson(objectMapper.writeValueAsString(buildManifest(entries)));
   292	        } catch (Exception e) {
   293	            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to serialize metadata", e);
   294	        }
   295	
   296	        version = skillVersionRepository.save(version);
   297	
   298	        // 9. Upload each file to storage and compute SHA-256
   299	        List<SkillFile> skillFiles = new ArrayList<>();
   300	        long totalSize = 0;
   301	
   302	        try {
   303	            MessageDigest digest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
   304	            HexFormat hexFormat = HexFormat.of();
   305	
   306	            for (PackageEntry entry : entries) {
   307	                String storageKey = String.format("skills/%d/%d/%s", skill.getId(), version.getId(), entry.path());
   308	
   309	                // Upload to storage
   310	                objectStorageService.putObject(
   311	                        storageKey,
   312	                        new ByteArrayInputStream(entry.content()),
   313	                        entry.size(),
   314	                        entry.contentType()
   315	                );
   316	
   317	                // Compute SHA-256
   318	                byte[] hash = digest.digest(entry.content());
   319	                String sha256 = hexFormat.formatHex(hash);
   320	
   321	                // Create SkillFile record
   322	                SkillFile skillFile = new SkillFile(
   323	                        version.getId(),
   324	                        entry.path(),
   325	                        entry.size(),
   326	                        entry.contentType(),
   327	                        sha256,
   328	                        storageKey
   329	                );
   330	                skillFiles.add(skillFile);
   331	                totalSize += entry.size();
   332	
   333	                digest.reset();
   334	            }
   335	        } catch (Exception e) {
   336	            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to process files", e);
   337	        }
   338	
   339	        // 10. Save SkillFile records
   340	        skillFileRepository.saveAll(skillFiles);
   341	
   342	        // 10.5 Build and upload bundle zip for download endpoints
   343	        byte[] bundleZip = buildBundle(entries);
   344	        String bundleKey = String.format("packages/%d/%d/bundle.zip", skill.getId(), version.getId());
   345	        objectStorageService.putObject(
   346	                bundleKey,
   347	                new ByteArrayInputStream(bundleZip),
   348	                bundleZip.length,
   349	                "application/zip"
   350	        );
   351	
   352	        // 11. Update version stats
   353	        version.setFileCount(skillFiles.size());
   354	        version.setTotalSize(totalSize);
   355	        version.setBundleReady(true);
   356	        version.setDownloadReady(!skillFiles.isEmpty());
   357	        skillVersionRepository.save(version);
   358	
   359	        if (!autoPublish) {
   360	            ReviewTask reviewTask = new ReviewTask(version.getId(), namespace.getId(), publisherId);
   361	            ReviewTask savedReviewTask = reviewTaskRepository.save(reviewTask);
   362	            eventPublisher.publishEvent(new ReviewSubmittedEvent(
   363	                    savedReviewTask.getId(),
   364	                    skill.getId(),
   365	                    version.getId(),
   366	                    savedReviewTask.getSubmittedBy(),
   367	                    savedReviewTask.getNamespaceId()
   368	            ));
   369	            if (securityScanService.isEnabled()) {
   370	                securityScanService.triggerScan(version.getId(), entries, publisherId);
   371	            }
   372	        }
   373	
   374	        // 12. Update skill metadata and move the published pointer for auto-publish flows
   375	        skill.setDisplayName(metadata.name());
   376	        skill.setSummary(metadata.description());
   377	        if (autoPublish) {
   378	            skill.setLatestVersionId(version.getId());
   379	            skill.setVisibility(visibility);
   380	        }
   381	        skill.setUpdatedBy(publisherId);
   382	        skillRepository.save(skill);
   383	
   384	        if (autoPublish) {
   385	            eventPublisher.publishEvent(new SkillPublishedEvent(skill.getId(), version.getId(), publisherId));
   386	        }
   387	
   388	        // 13. Return identifiers for the created version
   389	        return new PublishResult(skill.getId(), skill.getSlug(), version);
   390	    }
   391	
   392	    private void deleteReplaceableVersionArtifacts(Skill skill, SkillVersion version, String namespaceSlug) {
   393	        if (version.getStatus() == SkillVersionStatus.PUBLISHED) {
   394	            throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.skill.version.exists", version.getVersion());
   395	        }
   396	
   397	        reviewTaskRepository.findBySkillVersionIdAndStatus(version.getId(), ReviewTaskStatus.PENDING)
   398	                .ifPresent(reviewTaskRepository::delete);
   399	
   400	        List<SkillFile> files = skillFileRepository.findByVersionId(version.getId());
   401	        List<String> storageKeys = new ArrayList<>();
   402	        files.stream()
   403	                .map(SkillFile::getStorageKey)
   404	                .filter(key -> key != null && !key.isBlank())
   405	                .forEach(storageKeys::add);
   406	        storageKeys.add(buildBundleStorageKey(skill.getId(), version.getId()));
   407	        deleteStorageAfterCommit(skill, namespaceSlug, storageKeys);
   408	        skillFileRepository.deleteByVersionId(version.getId());
   409	        securityScanService.softDeleteByVersionId(version.getId());
   410	        skillVersionRepository.delete(version);
   411	        skillVersionRepository.flush();
   412	
   413	        if (version.getId().equals(skill.getLatestVersionId())) {
   414	            skill.setLatestVersionId(null);
   415	        }
   416	    }
   417	
   418	    private String resolveNamespaceSlug(Long namespaceId) {
   419	        return namespaceRepository.findById(namespaceId)
   420	                .orElseThrow(() -> new DomainBadRequestException("error.namespace.notFound", namespaceId))
   421	                .getSlug();
   422	    }
   423	
   424	    private void deleteStorageAfterCommit(Skill skill, String namespaceSlug, List<String> storageKeys) {
   425	        if (storageKeys.isEmpty()) {
   426	            return;
   427	        }
   428	        if (!TransactionSynchronizationManager.isSynchronizationActive()) {
   429	            deleteStorageWithCompensation(skill, namespaceSlug, storageKeys);
   430	            return;
   431	        }
   432	        TransactionSynchronizationManager.registerSynchronization(new TransactionSynchronization() {
   433	            @Override
   434	            public void afterCommit() {
   435	                deleteStorageWithCompensation(skill, namespaceSlug, storageKeys);
   436	            }
   437	        });
   438	    }
   439	
   440	    private void deleteStorageWithCompensation(Skill skill, String namespaceSlug, List<String> storageKeys) {
   441	        try {
   442	            objectStorageService.deleteObjects(storageKeys);
   443	        } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
   444	            compensationService.recordFailure(
   445	                    skill.getId(),
   446	                    namespaceSlug,
   447	                    skill.getSlug(),
   448	                    storageKeys,
   449	                    ex.getMessage()
   450	            );
   451	            log.error("Failed to delete replaced version storage after commit [skillId={}, versionKeys={}]",
   452	                    skill.getId(), storageKeys, ex);
   453	        }
   454	    }
   455	
   456	    private String buildBundleStorageKey(Long skillId, Long versionId) {
   457	        return String.format("packages/%d/%d/bundle.zip", skillId, versionId);
   458	    }
   459	
   460	    private void assertNamespaceWritable(Namespace namespace) {
   461	        if (namespace.getStatus() == NamespaceStatus.FROZEN) {
   462	            throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.namespace.frozen", namespace.getSlug());
   463	        }
   464	        if (namespace.getStatus() == NamespaceStatus.ARCHIVED) {
   465	            throw new DomainBadRequestException("error.namespace.archived", namespace.getSlug());
   466	        }
   467	    }
   468	
   469	    private void assertCanManageLifecycle(Skill skill,
   470	                                          String actorUserId,
   471	                                          Map<Long, NamespaceRole> userNamespaceRoles) {
   472	        NamespaceRole namespaceRole = userNamespaceRoles.get(skill.getNamespaceId());
   473	        boolean canManage = skill.getOwnerId().equals(actorUserId)
   474	                || namespaceRole == NamespaceRole.ADMIN
   475	                || namespaceRole == NamespaceRole.OWNER;
   476	        if (!canManage) {
   477	            throw new DomainForbiddenException("error.skill.lifecycle.noPermission");
   478	        }
   479	    }
   480	
   481	    private Instant currentTime() {
   482	        return Instant.now(clock);
   483	    }
   484	
   485	    private List<PackageEntry> rebuildEntriesForRerelease(Long skillId, Long versionId, String targetVersion) {
   486	        List<SkillFile> files = skillFileRepository.findByVersionId(versionId).stream()
   487	                .sorted(Comparator.comparing(SkillFile::getFilePath))
   488	                .toList();
   489	        List<PackageEntry> entries = new ArrayList<>(files.size());
   490	        for (SkillFile file : files) {
   491	            byte[] content = readAllBytes(objectStorageService.getObject(file.getStorageKey()));
   492	            if ("SKILL.md".equals(file.getFilePath())) {
   493	                content = rewriteSkillMdVersion(content, targetVersion);
   494	            }
   495	            entries.add(new PackageEntry(
   496	                    file.getFilePath(),
   497	                    content,
   498	                    content.length,
   499	                    file.getContentType() != null ? file.getContentType() : "application/octet-stream"
   500	            ));
   501	        }
   502	        return entries;
   503	    }
   504	
   505	    private byte[] readAllBytes(InputStream inputStream) {
   506	        try (InputStream in = inputStream) {
   507	            return in.readAllBytes();
   508	        } catch (IOException e) {
   509	            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to read stored skill file", e);
   510	        }
   511	    }
   512	
   513	    private byte[] rewriteSkillMdVersion(byte[] content, String targetVersion) {
   514	        String skillMdContent = new String(content);
   515	        SkillMetadata metadata = skillMetadataParser.parse(skillMdContent);
   516	        Map<String, Object> frontmatter = new LinkedHashMap<>(metadata.frontmatter());
   517	        frontmatter.put("version", targetVersion);
   518	        String rewritten = "---\n"
   519	                + new Yaml().dump(frontmatter).trim()
   520	                + "\n---\n"
   521	                + metadata.body();
   522	        return rewritten.getBytes();
   523	    }
   524	
   525	    private List<Map<String, Object>> buildManifest(List<PackageEntry> entries) {
   526	        return entries.stream()
   527	                .map(entry -> Map.<String, Object>of(
   528	                        "path", entry.path(),
   529	                        "size", entry.size(),
   530	                        "contentType", entry.contentType()))
   531	                .toList();
   532	    }
   533	
   534	    private byte[] buildBundle(List<PackageEntry> entries) {
   535	        try (ByteArrayOutputStream outputStream = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   536	             ZipOutputStream zipOutputStream = new ZipOutputStream(outputStream)) {
   537	            for (PackageEntry entry : entries) {
   538	                ZipEntry zipEntry = new ZipEntry(entry.path());
   539	                zipOutputStream.putNextEntry(zipEntry);
   540	                zipOutputStream.write(entry.content());
   541	                zipOutputStream.closeEntry();
   542	            }
   543	            zipOutputStream.finish();
   544	            return outputStream.toByteArray();
   545	        } catch (Exception e) {
   546	            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to build bundle zip", e);
   547	        }
   548	    }
   549	}

cat > /tmp/Reproduce2.java << 'EOF'
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Reproduce2 {
    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    );
    
    private static final Pattern SECRET_RULE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})"
    );
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String[] testCases = {
            // Should be caught (real secrets)
            "token = \"ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx\"",
            "api_key = \"sk-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx\"",
            "token=sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz123456",
            
            // Should NOT be caught (false positives from PR)
            "token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)",
            "requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)",
            "password = get_password()",
            "secret = some_variable_name",
            
            // Placeholders (should be filtered)
            "token=YOUR_TOKEN_HERE",
            "api_key=example-key-value",
        };
        
        for (String line : testCases) {
            Matcher matcher = SECRET_RULE.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            String status;
            if (found) {
                String value = matcher.group(2);
                if (isPlaceholderValue(value)) {
                    status = "MATCHED but filtered as placeholder: " + value;
                } else {
                    status = "MATCHED (ERROR): " + value;
                }
            } else {
                status = "NOT matched (OK)";
            }
            System.out.println(status + "  |  " + line);
        }
    }
    
    private static boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
            return false;
        }
        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    }
}
EOF

import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Reproduce3 {
    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    );
    
    private static final Pattern SECRET_RULE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})"
    );
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String[] testCases = {
            // Should be caught (real secrets)
            "token = \"ghp_12345678901234567890\"",
            "api_key = \"sk-12345678901234567890\"",
            "token=sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz",
            
            // Should NOT be caught (false positives from PR)
            "token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)",
            "requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)",
            "password = get_password_value_some()",
            "secret = some_long_variable_name",
            
            // Placeholders (should be filtered)
            "token=YOUR_TOKEN_HERE",
            "api_key=example-key-value",
        };
        
        for (String line : testCases) {
            Matcher matcher = SECRET_RULE.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            String status;
            if (found) {
                String value = matcher.group(2);
                if (isPlaceholderValue(value)) {
                    status = "MATCHED but filtered as placeholder: " + value;
                } else {
                    status = "MATCHED (ERROR): " + value;
                }
            } else {
                status = "NOT matched (OK)";
            }
            System.out.println(status + "  |  " + line);
        }
    }
    
    private static boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
            return false;
        }
        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    }
}

2026-05-30 02:03:13,438 - INFO - swea-agent-iflytek__skillhub-253 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I can clearly see the false positives. Let me now design the fix.

The key insight: the regex should not match when the "value" is actually a function call (followed by `(`) or when it's an unquoted identifier that looks like a variable reference.

But as I noted earlier, distinguishing between:
- `token = abcdefghijklm` (hardcoded secret)
- `token = some_long_variable_name` (variable reference)

is syntactically impossible without parsing the code.

However, looking at the PR description again:

> The validator should block obvious hardcoded credentials, but should not reject:
> - variable assignments
> - function-call return values
> - ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc.

The PR says that `token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)` should be allowed. This is a function call.

And `token = "ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"` should still fail. This is a quoted string.

But what about `token = some_hardcoded_secret_value`? Is that a variable reference or a hardcoded secret? In Python, it would be a NameError if `some_hardcoded_secret_value` is not defined, so it's unlikely to be intentional.

I think the pragmatic fix is:

1. Add `(?!\s*\()` to prevent matching function calls
2. For unquoted values, maybe require them to look more "secret-like" (contain numbers, mixed case, etc.)

But actually, let me look at this from another angle. The specific rules 1-3 already catch the most common secret patterns:
- AWS keys: `AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16}`
- GitHub tokens: `ghp_[A-Za-z0-9]{20,}`
- API keys: `sk-[A-Za-z0-9]{20,}`

Rule 4 is a catch-all. Maybe we should simply make rule 4 only match when the value is quoted? That would:
- Allow `token = extract_group_token_value(...)` (no quotes)
- Allow `token = some_variable` (no quotes)
- Catch `token = "hardcoded_secret_123"` (quoted)
- Catch `api_key: "my-secret-key"` (quoted)

But we'd miss `password = mySecretPassword` in a config file. However, the PR specifically says we should not reject "ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc."

Let me check if there are other test files that might have been updated for this PR:

- It still catches quoted string values
- It doesn't catch function calls (identifiers followed by `(`)
- It doesn't catch simple variable references (but this is harder)

**Option A**: Modify the regex to only match when the value is quoted, OR when the value is unquoted but followed by a word boundary and not `(`.

But wait, the current regex already optionally matches a quote: `['\"]?`. The problem is that it only matches the opening quote but doesn't require the closing quote or check what follows the value.

Let me try a different approach. Let me modify the regex to:

1. If quoted (opening quote present): match the value inside quotes, requiring the closing quote
2. If unquoted: match the value but ensure it's not followed by `(` or `.` (function calls and method chains)

Here's my proposed new regex:

```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*(?:['\"]([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})['\"]|(?!['\"])([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})(?!\s*\())
```

Wait, this is getting complex. Let me simplify.

Actually, I think the simplest effective fix is to add a negative lookahead after the value group to ensure it's not a function call. And also, if the value is unquoted, we should ensure it's not just a plain identifier by checking if it ends at a proper boundary.

But the PR also says "ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc." should be allowed. So maybe we should ONLY flag quoted values in rule 4 (since rules 1-3 handle specific unquoted patterns).

Let me go with this approach: modify the regex to require quotes around the value. If someone writes `token = "someSecretValue123"`, it will be caught. If they write `token = some_function()`, it won't match because there are no quotes.

```

Let me verify: `sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz123456` - does it match rule 3?

So yes, the existing test would still pass even if we modify rule 4.

Now, let me think about edge cases:
- `password = "correct horse battery staple"` - this has spaces, won't match the character class
- `token: "ya29.a0AfH6..."` - Google token with dots, won't match
- `secret = "my-secret-123456789012"` - 23 chars with dashes, would match (good)

```

```

New:

```

But our character class doesn't include `'`, so it would stop before the `'`. Actually, `"value's"` - the regex would match `"` then `value` (5 chars, too short) then `s` is not a quote... hmm, this is tricky.

Let me think more carefully. The current regex `['\"]?` optionally matches a single quote. If we make it mandatory, we need to handle both `"..."` and `'...'`.

My proposed regex:
```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*(?:'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})'|\"([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})\")
```

This uses alternation to match either single-quoted or double-quoted values. The value group number changes depending on which alternative matches. This would require changing the `valueGroup` in the `SecretRule` constructor.

But actually, looking at the code, `matcher.group(rule.valueGroup())` is used to get the value. If we have two capturing groups for the value (one for single quotes, one for double quotes), we'd need to handle that.

A simpler approach: keep the optional quote for the opening, but add a requirement that if there was an opening quote, there must be a closing quote, and if there was no opening quote, the value must not be followed by `(`.

But this is getting complex. Let me look at this differently.

Actually, maybe the simplest fix is:
1. Keep the regex mostly the same
2. Add a negative lookahead `(?!\s*\()` after the value group to prevent matching function calls
3. For unquoted values that are just identifiers, rely on the fact that real secrets usually have specific patterns (caught by rules 1-3) or are quoted

Let me test this approach:

```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})(?!\s*\()

cat > /tmp/Reproduce4.java << 'EOF'
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Reproduce4 {
    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    );
    
    // NEW regex with negative lookahead for (
    private static final Pattern SECRET_RULE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})(?!\\s*\\()"
    );
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String[] testCases = {
            // Should be caught (real secrets)
            "token = \"ghp_12345678901234567890\"",
            "api_key = \"sk-12345678901234567890\"",
            "token=sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz",
            
            // Should NOT be caught (false positives from PR)
            "token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)",
            "requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)",
            "password = get_password_value_some()",
            "secret = some_long_variable_name",
            
            // Placeholders (should be filtered)
            "token=YOUR_TOKEN_HERE",
            "api_key=example-key-value",
            
            // Additional edge cases
            "token = some_func()",
            "password = \"mySecretPassword123\"",
            "secret: \"abcdefghijklm\"",
        };
        
        for (String line : testCases) {
            Matcher matcher = SECRET_RULE.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            String status;
            if (found) {
                String value = matcher.group(2);
                if (isPlaceholderValue(value)) {
                    status = "MATCHED but filtered as placeholder: " + value;
                } else {
                    status = "MATCHED (ERROR): " + value;
                }
            } else {
                status = "NOT matched (OK)";
            }
            System.out.println(status + "  |  " + line);
        }
    }
    
    private static boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
            return false;
        }
        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    }
}

`extract_group_token_value` - let me count: e-x-t-r-a-c-t-_-g-r-o-u-p-_-t-o-k-e-n-_-v-a-l-u-e = 24 characters. Wait: e(1) x(2) t(3) r(4) a(5) c(6) t(7) _(8) g(9) r(10) o(11) u(12) p(13) _(14) t(15) o(16) k(17) e(18) n(19) _(20) v(21) a(22) l(23) u(24) e(25) = 25 characters.

So the regex captures 25 chars: `extract_group_token_value`. But the output says `extract_group_token_valu` (missing 'e'). Let me check why the lookahead isn't working.

Oh wait, the output says `extract_group_token_valu` - it's missing the last `e`. Let me check the character class: `[A-Za-z0-9_\-]`. The `e` should be included. But the match shows `extract_group_token_valu`. 

Oh! I think the issue is that the regex is matching but the negative lookahead `(?!\s*\()` is checking AFTER the 12+ characters. Since `extract_group_token_value` is 25 characters, and after it comes `(response...`, the lookahead sees `(` (with possible whitespace before it) and should reject the match. But it seems like the regex engine might be backtracking.

Wait, let me re-examine. The regex `([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})(?!\s*\()` - the `{12,}` is greedy, so it tries to match as many characters as possible. It matches all 25 chars of `extract_group_token_value`, then checks `(?!\s*\()` which sees `(response...` - the next char is `(`, so the lookahead FAILS. Then the regex backtracks: it tries matching 24 chars (`extract_group_token_valu`), then checks `(?!\s*\()` - the next char is `e`, not `(`, so the lookahead SUCCEEDS. That's why it matches `extract_group_token_valu` (24 chars) instead of the full 25.

So the negative lookahead approach partially works but has a flaw: it backtracks to a shorter match that doesn't have `(` after it. We need to prevent this backtracking.

A better approach: use a possessive quantifier or an atomic group to prevent backtracking, OR use a different strategy.

Let me try using `(?>...)` atomic group or `{12,}+` possessive quantifier:

Actually, Java supports possessive quantifiers. Let me try `{12,}+`:

```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,}+)(?!\s*\()
```

The `+` after `{12,}` makes it possessive, meaning it won't backtrack

cat > /tmp/Reproduce5.java << 'EOF'
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Reproduce5 {
    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    );
    
    // NEW regex with possessive quantifier and negative lookahead
    private static final Pattern SECRET_RULE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,}+)(?!\\s*\\()"
    );
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String[] testCases = {
            // Should be caught (real secrets)
            "token = \"ghp_12345678901234567890\"",
            "api_key = \"sk-12345678901234567890\"",
            "token=sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz",
            
            // Should NOT be caught (false positives from PR)
            "token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)",
            "requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)",
            "password = get_password_value_some()",
            "secret = some_long_variable_name",
            
            // Placeholders (should be filtered)
            "token=YOUR_TOKEN_HERE",
            "api_key=example-key-value",
            
            // Additional edge cases
            "token = some_func()",
            "password = \"mySecretPassword123\"",
            "secret: \"abcdefghijklm\"",
            "api_key = 'sk-12345678901234567890'",
        };
        
        for (String line : testCases) {
            Matcher matcher = SECRET_RULE.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            String status;
            if (found) {
                String value = matcher.group(2);
                if (isPlaceholderValue(value)) {
                    status = "MATCHED but filtered as placeholder: " + value;
                } else {
                    status = "MATCHED (ERROR): " + value;
                }
            } else {
                status = "NOT matched (OK)";
            }
            System.out.println(status + "  |  " + line);
        }
    }
    
    private static boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
            return false;
        }
        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    }
}

Now the function calls are correctly rejected. But `secret = some_long_variable_name` is still matched. As I mentioned earlier, this is hard to distinguish from a real hardcoded secret without parsing.

But wait, the PR says:
> - variable assignments
> - function-call return values
> - ordinary identifiers that happen to contain words like token, secret, etc.

All of these should be allowed. `secret = some_long_variable_name` is a variable assignment (assigning one variable to another). It should be allowed.

So how do we handle this? If we can't distinguish between:
- `secret = some_long_variable_name` (variable reference, should be allowed)
- `secret = mySecretValue123` (hardcoded secret, should be caught)

...then maybe we should only flag quoted values in rule 4?

Let me check: what kind of unquoted hardcoded secrets would rule 4 need to catch that rules 1-3 don't already catch?

Rules 1-3 catch:
- `AKIA...` (AWS access keys)
- `ghp_...` (GitHub tokens)
- `sk-...` (API keys)

Rule 4 would catch things like:
- `password = mySecretPassword123`
- `secret = abcdefghijklmnop`
- `token = someRandomToken123`

But these could also be variable names. The distinction is really hard without parsing.

I think the PR's intent is clear: rule 4 should only catch quoted string literals, because unquoted values are ambiguous (could be variable references or function calls). The specific patterns (rules 1-3) handle well-known secret formats.

So my final approach: modify rule 4 to require quotes around the value. Let me implement this.

New regex:
```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*['\"]([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})['\"]
```

But this requires the same quote character for both opening and closing. Let me handle both quote styles:

Actually, let me use a backreference to ensure the same quote is used:
```
(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\s*[:=]\s*(['\"])([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})\2
```

Here `\2` refers to the captured quote character. Now the valueGroup would be 3.

Let me test this:



🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/Reproduce6.java << 'EOF'
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Reproduce6 {
    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    );
    
    // NEW regex requiring quotes
    private static final Pattern SECRET_RULE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*(['\\\"])([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})\\2"
    );
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String[] testCases = {
            // Should be caught (real secrets) - QUOTED
            "token = \"ghp_12345678901234567890\"",
            "api_key = \"sk-12345678901234567890\"",
            "api_key = 'sk-12345678901234567890'",
            "password = \"mySecretPassword123\"",
            "secret: \"abcdefghijklm\"",
            
            // Should NOT be caught - UNQUOTED (but rule 3 catches sk-...)
            "token=sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz",
            
            // Should NOT be caught (false positives from PR)
            "token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)",
            "requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)",
            "password = get_password_value_some()",
            "secret = some_long_variable_name",
            "token = some_func()",
            
            // Placeholders (should be filtered)
            "token=\"YOUR_TOKEN_HERE\"",
            "api_key=\"example-key-value\"",
        };
        
        for (String line : testCases) {
            Matcher matcher = SECRET_RULE.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            String status;
            if (found) {
                String value = matcher.group(3);  // valueGroup is now 3
                if (isPlaceholderValue(value)) {
                    status = "MATCHED but filtered as placeholder: " + value;
                } else {
                    status = "MATCHED (ERROR): " + value;
                }
            } else {
                status = "NOT matched (OK)";
            }
            System.out.println(status + "  |  " + line);
        }
    }
    
    private static boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
            return false;
        }
        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    }
}
EOF

     1	package com.iflytek.skillhub.domain.skill.validation;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     4	
     5	import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
     6	import java.util.ArrayList;
     7	import java.util.List;
     8	import java.util.Locale;
     9	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    10	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    11	
    12	/**
    13	 * Default pre-publish validator that scans text-like package files for likely secrets and
    14	 * accidental real credentials.
    15	 */
    16	@Component
    17	public class BasicPrePublishValidator implements PrePublishValidator {
    18	
    19	    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
    20	            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    21	    );
    22	    private static final List<SecretRule> SECRET_RULES = List.of(
    23	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16})"), 1, "cloud access key"),
    24	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(ghp_[A-Za-z0-9]{20,})"), 1, "GitHub token"),
    25	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(sk-[A-Za-z0-9]{20,})"), 1, "API key"),
    26	            new SecretRule(
    27	                    Pattern.compile("(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*['\\\"]?([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})"),
    28	                    2,
    29	                    "secret or token")
    30	    );
    31	
    32	    @Override
    33	    public ValidationResult validate(SkillPackageContext context) {
    34	        List<String> errors = new ArrayList<>();
    35	
    36	        for (PackageEntry entry : context.entries()) {
    37	            if (!isTextLike(entry.path())) {
    38	                continue;
    39	            }
    40	            String content = new String(entry.content(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    41	            String[] lines = content.split("\\R", -1);
    42	            for (int i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    43	                String line = lines[i];
    44	                for (SecretRule rule : SECRET_RULES) {
    45	                    Matcher matcher = rule.pattern().matcher(line);
    46	                    if (!matcher.find()) {
    47	                        continue;
    48	                    }
    49	                    String matchedValue = matcher.group(rule.valueGroup());
    50	                    if (isPlaceholderValue(matchedValue)) {
    51	                        continue;
    52	                    }
    53	                    errors.add(entry.path()
    54	                            + " line " + (i + 1)
    55	                            + " contains a value that looks like a "
    56	                            + rule.label()
    57	                            + ". Replace real credentials with placeholders before publishing.");
    58	                    break;
    59	                }
    60	            }
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        return errors.isEmpty() ? ValidationResult.pass() : ValidationResult.fail(errors);
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    private boolean isTextLike(String path) {
    67	        String lowerPath = path.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    68	        return lowerPath.endsWith(".md") || lowerPath.endsWith(".txt")
    69	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".json") || lowerPath.endsWith(".yaml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".yml")
    70	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".js") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ts")
    71	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".py") || lowerPath.endsWith(".sh") || lowerPath.endsWith(".svg")
    72	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".html") || lowerPath.endsWith(".css") || lowerPath.endsWith(".csv")
    73	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".toml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".xml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ini")
    74	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".cfg") || lowerPath.endsWith(".env")
    75	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".rb") || lowerPath.endsWith(".go") || lowerPath.endsWith(".rs")
    76	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".java") || lowerPath.endsWith(".kt") || lowerPath.endsWith(".lua")
    77	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".sql") || lowerPath.endsWith(".r")
    78	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".bat") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ps1")
    79	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".zsh") || lowerPath.endsWith(".bash");
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    private boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
    83	        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
    84	            return false;
    85	        }
    86	        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
    87	                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    private record SecretRule(Pattern pattern, int valueGroup, String label) {}
    91	}

     8	import java.util.Locale;
     9	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    10	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    11	
    12	/**
    13	 * Default pre-publish validator that scans text-like package files for likely secrets and
    14	 * accidental real credentials.
    15	 */
    16	@Component
    17	public class BasicPrePublishValidator implements PrePublishValidator {
    18	
    19	    private static final Pattern PLACEHOLDER_VALUE = Pattern.compile(
    20	            "(?i).*(your|example|sample|placeholder|changeme|replace|dummy|mock|test|fake|todo|xxx|redacted).*"
    21	    );
    22	    private static final List<SecretRule> SECRET_RULES = List.of(
    23	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16})"), 1, "cloud access key"),
    24	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(ghp_[A-Za-z0-9]{20,})"), 1, "GitHub token"),
    25	            new SecretRule(Pattern.compile("(sk-[A-Za-z0-9]{20,})"), 1, "API key"),
    26	            new SecretRule(
    27	                    Pattern.compile("(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*(['\\\"])([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})\\2"),
    28	                    2,
    29	                    "secret or token")
    30	    );
    31	
    32	    @Override
    33	    public ValidationResult validate(SkillPackageContext context) {
    34	        List<String> errors = new ArrayList<>();
    35	
    36	        for (PackageEntry entry : context.entries()) {
    37	            if (!isTextLike(entry.path())) {
    38	                continue;
    39	            }
    40	            String content = new String(entry.content(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    41	            String[] lines = content.split("\\R", -1);
    42	            for (int i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    43	                String line = lines[i];
    44	                for (SecretRule rule : SECRET_RULES) {
    45	                    Matcher matcher = rule.pattern().matcher(line);
    46	                    if (!matcher.find()) {
    47	                        continue;
    48	                    }
    49	                    String matchedValue = matcher.group(rule.valueGroup());
    50	                    if (isPlaceholderValue(matchedValue)) {
    51	                        continue;
    52	                    }
    53	                    errors.add(entry.path()
    54	                            + " line " + (i + 1)
    55	                            + " contains a value that looks like a "
    56	                            + rule.label()
    57	                            + ". Replace real credentials with placeholders before publishing.");
    58	                    break;
    59	                }
    60	            }
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        return errors.isEmpty() ? ValidationResult.pass() : ValidationResult.fail(errors);
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    private boolean isTextLike(String path) {
    67	        String lowerPath = path.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    68	        return lowerPath.endsWith(".md") || lowerPath.endsWith(".txt")
    69	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".json") || lowerPath.endsWith(".yaml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".yml")
    70	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".js") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ts")
    71	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".py") || lowerPath.endsWith(".sh") || lowerPath.endsWith(".svg")
    72	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".html") || lowerPath.endsWith(".css") || lowerPath.endsWith(".csv")
    73	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".toml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".xml") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ini")
    74	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".cfg") || lowerPath.endsWith(".env")
    75	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".rb") || lowerPath.endsWith(".go") || lowerPath.endsWith(".rs")
    76	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".java") || lowerPath.endsWith(".kt") || lowerPath.endsWith(".lua")
    77	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".sql") || lowerPath.endsWith(".r")
    78	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".bat") || lowerPath.endsWith(".ps1")
    79	                || lowerPath.endsWith(".zsh") || lowerPath.endsWith(".bash");
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    private boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
    83	        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
    84	            return false;
    85	        }
    86	        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
    87	                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    private record SecretRule(Pattern pattern, int valueGroup, String label) {}
    91	}

    // The new regex from the file
    private static final Pattern SECRET_RULE = Pattern.compile(
            "(?i)(api[_-]?key|access[_-]?key|secret|password|token)\\s*[:=]\\s*(['\\\"])([A-Za-z0-9_\\-]{12,})\\2"
    );
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String[][] testCases = {
            // {line, should_match, description}
            {"token = \"ghp_12345678901234567890\"", "true", "quoted secret - should catch"},
            {"api_key = \"sk-12345678901234567890\"", "true", "quoted API key - should catch"},
            {"api_key = 'sk-12345678901234567890'", "true", "single-quoted API key - should catch"},
            {"password = \"mySecretPassword123\"", "true", "quoted password - should catch"},
            {"secret: \"abcdefghijklm\"", "true", "YAML-style quoted secret - should catch"},
            
            // Should NOT be caught
            {"token=sk-abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz", "false", "unquoted sk- token (caught by rule 3)"},
            {"token = extract_group_token_value(response, group_choice.group_id)", "false", "function call - should NOT catch"},
            {"requested_token = secrets.token_hex(20)", "false", "function call - should NOT catch"},
            {"password = get_password_value_some()", "false", "function call - should NOT catch"},
            {"secret = some_long_variable_name", "false", "variable reference - should NOT catch"},
            {"token = some_func()", "false", "short function call - should NOT catch"},
            
            // Placeholders
            {"token=\"YOUR_TOKEN_HERE\"", "true", "placeholder - should be caught by regex but filtered"},
            {"api_key=\"example-key-value\"", "true", "placeholder - should be caught by regex but filtered"},
            
            // Edge cases
            {"token = \"short\"", "false", "too short - should NOT catch"},
            {"token = \"123456789012\"", "true", "exactly 12 chars - should catch"},
            {"password: \"mixed-dashes_underscores\"", "false", "only 24? let me count..."},
        };
        
        for (String[] test : testCases) {
            String line = test[0];
            boolean shouldMatch = Boolean.parseBoolean(test[1]);
            String desc = test[2];
            
            Matcher matcher = SECRET_RULE.matcher(line);
            boolean found = matcher.find();
            
            String status;
            if (found) {
                String value = matcher.group(3);  // valueGroup is 3
                if (isPlaceholderValue(value)) {
                    status = "MATCH_BUT_PLACEHOLDER";
                } else {
                    status = "MATCH";
                }
            } else {
                status = "NO_MATCH";
            }
            
            boolean pass = (found && shouldMatch) || (!found && !shouldMatch);
            System.out.println((pass ? "PASS" : "FAIL") + " | " + status + " | " + desc + " | " + line);
        }
    }
    
    private static boolean isPlaceholderValue(String value) {
        if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
            return false;
        }
        return PLACEHOLDER_VALUE.matcher(value).matches()
                || value.chars().allMatch(ch -> ch == 'x' || ch == 'X' || ch == '*' || ch == '-');
    }
}

- `\\s` → `\s` (whitespace)
- `\\2` → `\2` (backreference to group 2)

- `['` - start of character class with single quote
- `\\\"` - this is: `\\` (backslash) + `\"` (escaped double quote) = `\"` in the regex
- `]` - end of character class

- `\"` - one double quote in regex (escaped double quote in Java)  
- `]?` - literal `]?`

So the actual regex is: `['\"]?` which matches optional `'` or `"`.

"(['\\\"])"
```
Same breakdown:
- `(['` - literal `(['`
- `\\` - backslash in regex
- `\"` - double quote in regex
- `])` - literal `])`

So the regex is: `(['\"])` which captures `'` or `"`. And then `\\2` in Java becomes `\2` in regex, which backreferences the captured quote. This is correct!

- `\\-` → `\-` in regex, which is an escaped hyphen matching literal `-`

This is correct.

Now, I'm concerned about one more edge case: what if there are spaces between the value and the closing quote? Like `token = "mySecretValue123" `. The regex `(['\"])([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{12,})\2` requires the closing quote immediately after the value. But if there's a space like `"mySecretValue123" `, it still works because the value is `mySecretValue123` and the closing quote `"` follows immediately.

What about `token = "mySecret Value 123"`? The space would break the match because `[A-Za-z0-9_\-]` doesn't include space. So it wouldn't match. That's fine - such values are less likely to be secrets and more likely to be natural language.

Now let me also think about another approach that might be more robust. Instead of changing the regex, maybe I could add a post-match check in the code. But the PR description specifically mentions the regex as the issue, so fixing the regex is the right approach.
